class="expanded-review-7393563 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Currently, I programms"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Impact.com has few high quality programm like Canva, Hubspot, buzzsumo... but too few challengers solutions to promote.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">As an affiliate, it is easy to use, and the reporting is clear, and really easy of use.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">Unlike others plateforms partners stacks, it is hard to create your own links (ex: link to a specific page) <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Is is lacking of high quality partners. It is very limited if you want to promote lots of brands. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7060908 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I wanted to promote some brands, and Impact was the affiliate plateform used by these brands <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more
